Expand the middle term:
\[
=11.119\,\epsilon^2 + 11.119\,\epsilon \;-\;(11.119\cdot 0.091956)\,\epsilon\,(T-352.008)\;+\;4.3699\,(T-352.008)\log(\epsilon+1).
\]
So GT is a linear combination of these independent components:
- \(\epsilon^2\)
- \(\epsilon\)
- \(\epsilon\,T\) (equivalently \(\epsilon\,(T-352.008)\))
- \((T-352.008)\log(\epsilon+1)\) (i.e., \(T\log(\epsilon+1)\) plus a \(\log(\epsilon+1)\) term)

Crucially: GT has **no** \(\sqrt{T}\), **no** \(\exp(T\cdot)\), **no** trig in \(\epsilon\) or \(T\), and the only log is \(\log(\epsilon+1)\) multiplied by an affine function of \(T\).

Now check candidates for whether they can be tuned (by setting their free constants) to produce exactly that structure for all \(\epsilon\ge 0\) (relaxed domain) and all relevant \(T\).

GT Equivalence Verification (MatSci28)

GT: c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon*(-c3*(T - c4) + c5) + c6*(T - c7)*log(epsilon + c8)

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `11.119*epsilon^2 + 11.119*epsilon*(-0.0920*(T - 352.008) + 1) + 4.370*(T - 352.008)*log(epsilon + 1)`

Let me expand the GT:
- `11.119*epsilon^2 + 11.119*epsilon*(-0.0920*T + 32.384 + 1) + 4.370*(T - 352.008)*log(epsilon + 1)`
- `= 11.119*epsilon^2 + 11.119*epsilon*(-0.0920*T + 33.384) + 4.370*(T - 352.008)*log(epsilon + 1)`
- `= 11.119*epsilon^2 - 1.0226*T*epsilon + 371.22*epsilon + 4.370*T*log(epsilon+1) - 1538.3*log(epsilon+1)`

So GT has these basis function terms:
1. `epsilon^2`
2. `T*epsilon`
3. `epsilon`
4. `T*log(epsilon+1)`
5. `log(epsilon+1)`

This is a specific combination of basis functions. Let me check each candidate.

**Candidate 1:** `sqrt(T)*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2*exp(T*c3) + c4 + c5*log(c6*sin(c7*log(c8*epsilon+1)+c9)+1)`
Contains `sqrt(T)` and `exp(T*c3)` - these can't produce `T*epsilon` or `T*log(epsilon+1)`. Setting c3=0 makes exp constant, but then no T dependence in the log term. No way to get `T*epsilon` or `T*log(epsilon+1)`.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*log(c5*exp(T*c6)*|c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9)|+1)`
The last term involves log of exp(T*c6)*|sin(...)| + 1. This can't separate into T*log(epsilon+1) and T*epsilon cleanly.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*sin(c1+c2*sqrt(epsilon)) + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*exp(T^c6*c7)*log(c8*epsilon+1)`
Has sin(sqrt(epsilon)) which is not in GT. The exp(T^c6*c7) term - if c6=1, gives exp(T*c7)*log(c8*epsilon+1), which is exponential in T, not linear. Can't match.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*sin(c1+c2*sqrt(epsilon)) + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*exp(T*c6)*log(c7*epsilon+1)`
Same issue - sin(sqrt(epsilon)) and exp(T) can't produce the GT terms.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `T*c0*sin(c1+c2*sqrt(epsilon))/(T+c3) + T*c4*epsilon/(T+c3) + T*c5/(T+c3) + c6/(T+c3) + c7*sin(c1+c2*sqrt(epsilon))/(T+c3) + c8*epsilon/(T+c3) + c9*epsilon/(T+c3)`

Everything divided by (T+c3). Combining: `[T*c0*sin(...) + c7*sin(...) + T*c4*epsilon + (c8+c9)*epsilon + T*c5 + c6] / (T+c3)`

This equals `[(T+c3)*c0*sin(...) + (c7-c0*c3)*sin(...) + (T+c3)*c4*epsilon + (c8+c9-c4*c3)*epsilon + ...] / (T+c3)`

= `c0*sin(...) + c4*epsilon + c5 + [stuff]/(T+c3)`

This gives terms like sin(c1+c2*sqrt(epsilon)) which aren't in GT. No epsilon^2 or T*log(epsilon+1).
